After their mother is killed in an American firebombing raid and their father is missing in action serving in the Imperial Navy, the children are left to fend for themselves. ↵ Interestingly, director Isao Takahata often resisted the "anti-war" label. He intended the film to be a social critique of the isolation and pride of youth. He wanted to show how Seita’s decision to cut themselves off from society (by leaving their aunt's home to live alone) ultimately led to their tragedy. He felt that by isolating themselves, they lost the community support necessary for survival in such a brutal era. Id X

Easy for his systems to hit 99% accuracy when symptoms are neatly catecategorized in a spreadsheet. As the original phrase propagated into common parlance it was distorted due to different accents and dialects into its modern form XY. [2026-01-17T16:24:33Z] AntNishu: Q1: X fishing is an ancient Chinese technique, traceable to the Sui (6th century CE) dynasty, in which trained X catch fish for fishermen by diving, seizing fish, returning to the bamboo rafts, and releasing the catch on command, guided by whistles or calls. Fishermen often regard X as family members, reflecting a deep relational bond. ↵ Deeply fascinated by the practice, King James I of England institutionalised it by creating the official court position of Master of the Royal X for fishing on the Thames, transforming an asian subsistence technique into an aristocratic sport. ↵ With the advent of modern nets and industrial fishing, X fishing has become commercially obsolete. Today, it survives mainly on China's Li River, performed by elderly masters for visitors, enduring as a living symbol of China’s philosophy of human-nature harmony. ↵ ID X
